*Q1.* 📈 Who has MORE shells? Sia: 🐚🐚🐚🐚🐚🐚🐚🐚  |  Anaya: 🐚🐚🐚🐚🐚🐚🐚🐚🐚

B) Both same
C) Anaya
D) Sia
✅ *Answer:* C) Anaya
💡 9 is more than 8.
━━━━━━━━━━

*Q8.* ⚖️ Aman puts a drum of water and a cup on a seesaw.
A) A cup
B) A drum of water
C) Same weight
D) Cannot say
✅ *Answer:* B) A drum of water
💡 A drum of water is heavier than a cup.
